The hotel environment is very good, full of green, the air is great, and it is very quiet. It is very comfortable to take a walk after dinner.
The hotel is only a 14-minute walk from Zhaisha Dong Village, and it is also very convenient to walk there for a meal.
The hotel provides a pick-up service for Fanjing Mountain. When you check in, you can make an appoin**ent for the departure time the next day. If you call the hotel when you go down the mountain, you will pick it up.
In addition, if you are not driving by yourself, the passenger transport center is opposite the high-speed rail at Tongren Station. You can tell the driver that the bus will drop you off when it passes by the hotel; there are also buses from Fanjing Mountain Scenic Area that go directly to Tongren Station, which is super convenient!

msg:As a famous tourist attraction in Guizhou, Fanjing Mountain has good supporting facilities. I don't like to live in a bed and breakfast. I accidentally found this fairy hotel for me.

The hotel is located at Fanjingshan No. 2 parking lot, 3km away from the east gate. The hotel picks up customers to the entrance of the attraction for free. The shuttle bus is a GL8 commercial vehicle. It is really on-call without any delay. You need to know the parking fee of the Fanjingshan parking lot. : 35/time.

Upgrade to a deluxe mountain view room, the elegant room originally booked, 390/night, including two breakfasts. The hotel room is large, very quiet and soundproof. The bathroom is separated from wet and dry, and the shower room is very comfortable under the sunlight by the window.

I had a good breakfast. I had a bowl of egg rice noodles, which was especially delicious. The fruit was Chinese and Western, yogurt and coffee bean syrup, and my favorite Guizhou rice noodles. After filling my stomach, I went hiking.

The hotel's Chinese restaurant dishes are also highly recommended. The service is good, and the per capita is not 100. We ate here for dinner. The next day after climbing the mountain, we came back at more than 2 o'clock in the afternoon. We continued our lunch here. I was hungry and fainted.

The hotel is divided into three building areas. The lobby is particularly beautiful, with transparent floor-to-ceiling glass windows and large terraces. In short, no dissatisfaction can be found.
